<td align="left" valign="top" width="98%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; COLOR: #808080; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Principal at Risk Securities</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="98%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">The Trigger PLUS are senior unsecured obligations of Royal Bank of Canada, do not pay interest, do not guarantee any return of principal at maturity and have the terms described in the accompanying prospectus supplement and prospectus, as supplemented or modified by this document.&#160;&#160;At maturity, if the level of the underlying index has <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">increased</font>, investors will receive the stated principal amount of their investment plus a return reflecting the leveraged upside performance of the underlying index, subject to the maximum payment at maturity.&#160;&#160;However, at maturity, if the underlying index <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">does not change or has depreciated</font>, (i) if the level of the underlying index is greater than or equal to the trigger level, investors will receive the stated principal amount of their investment, or (ii) if the level of the underlying index is less than the trigger level, investors will lose 1% for every 1% decline in the underlying index from the pricing date to the valuation date.&#160;&#160;The Trigger PLUS are for investors who seek an equity index-based return and who are willing to risk their principal and forgo current income and upside above the maximum payment at maturity in exchange for the upside leverage feature and the limited protection against loss .&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Investors may lose their entire initial investment in the Trigger PLUS</font>.&#160;&#160;The Trigger PLUS are senior notes issued as part of Royal Bank of Canada&#8217;s Global Medium-Term Notes, Series F program.&#160;&#160;All payments on the Trigger PLUS are subject to the credit risk of Royal Bank of Canada.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

</td>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">To avoid loss in the event of a decline of the underlying index as of the valuation date, but only if the final index level is greater than or equal to the trigger level.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The Trigger PLUS are exposed on a 1:1 basis to the negative performance of the underlying index if the final index level is less than the trigger level.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 11pt">Trigger PLUS Based on the Performance of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index, due April 4, 2017</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #808080; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trigger Performance Leveraged Upside Securities<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">SM</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #808080; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Principal at Risk Securities</font></div>
</td>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 16pt">Key Investment Rationale</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">These Trigger PLUS offer leveraged exposure to the performance of the underlying index.&#160;&#160;In exchange for enhanced performance of 200% of the appreciation of the underlying index, investors forgo performance above the maximum payment at maturity of $12.55 per Trigger PLUS and are exposed to the risk of loss of all or a significant portion of their investment.&#160;&#160;At maturity, if the level of the underlying index has <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">increased</font>, investors will receive the stated principal amount of their investment plus a return reflecting the leveraged upside performance of the underlying index, subject to the maximum payment at maturity.&#160;&#160;However, at maturity, if the underlying index <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">does not change or has depreciated</font>, (i) if the level of the underlying index is greater than or equal to the trigger level, investors will receive the stated principal amount of their investment, or (ii) if the level of the underlying index is less than the trigger level, investors will lose 1% for every 1% decline in the underlying index from the pricing date to the valuation date.&#160;&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Investors may lose their entire initial investment in the Trigger PLUS.</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div align="left">
<table cellpadding="3" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Leveraged</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Performance</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="68%" style="BORDER-LEFT: #ffffff 1.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The Trigger PLUS offer investors an opportunity to capture enhanced returns relative to a direct investment in the underlying index within a certain range of positive performance.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>
</td>
</tr><tr>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="16%" bgcolor="#dcebf4" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: #ffffff 1.5pt solid; BORDER-LEFT: #ffffff 1.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trigger Feature</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="68%" style="BORDER-LEFT: #ffffff 1.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">At maturity, even if the underlying index has declined over the term of the Trigger PLUS, you will receive your stated principal amount, but only if the final index level is greater than or equal to the trigger level.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>
</td>
</tr><tr>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="16%" bgcolor="#dcebf4" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: #ffffff 1.5pt solid; BORDER-LEFT: #ffffff 1.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Upside Scenario</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="68%" style="BORDER-LEFT: #ffffff 1.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The level of the underlying index increases and, at maturity, we will pay the stated principal amount of $10 plus 200% of the underlying index return, subject to the maximum payment at maturity of $12.55 per Trigger PLUS (125.50% of the stated principal amount)<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman, serif">.</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>
</td>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="68%" style="BORDER-LEFT: #ffffff 1.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The level of the underlying index does not change or declines but the final index level is greater than or equal to the trigger level and, at maturity, we will pay the stated principal amount of $10 per Trigger PLUS<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman, serif">.</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="68%" style="BORDER-LEFT: #ffffff 1.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The level of the underlying index declines and the final index level is less than the trigger level and, at maturity<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman, serif">,</font> for each Trigger PLUS, we will pay an amount that is less than the stated principal amount by an amount that is proportionate to the full decline in the level of the underlying index.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 11pt">Trigger PLUS Based on the Performance of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index, due April 4, 2017</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #808080; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trigger Performance Leveraged Upside Securities<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">SM</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #808080; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Principal at Risk Securities</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 16pt">How the Trigger PLUS Work</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Payoff Diagram</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The payoff diagram below illustrates the payment at maturity on the Trigger PLUS for a range of hypothetical percentage changes in the level of the underlying index. The graph is based on the following terms:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr>
<td valign="top" width="10%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="25%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Stated principal amount:</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" colspan="2" valign="top" width="43%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">$10 per Trigger PLUS</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr>
<td valign="top" width="10%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="25%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Leverage factor:</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" colspan="2" valign="top" width="43%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">200%</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr>
<td valign="top" width="10%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="25%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Maximum payment at maturity:</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" colspan="2" valign="top" width="43%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">$12.55 per Trigger PLUS (125.50% of the stated principal amount)</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr>
<td valign="top" width="10%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="25%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trigger level:</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" colspan="2" valign="top" width="43%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">90% of the initial index level</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<div align="center">&#160;</div>

<div align="center">
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="90%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr>
<td valign="middle" width="71%" bgcolor="#dcebf4">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trigger PLUS Payoff Diagram</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr>
<td valign="middle" width="71%" style="BORDER-BOTTOM: black 0.5pt solid">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><img src="chart1.jpg" alt=""></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 11pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">How it works</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Upside Scenario.</font>&#160;&#160;If the final index level is greater than the initial index level, then investors would receive the $10 stated principal amount plus a return reflecting 200% of the appreciation of the underlying index over the term of the Trigger PLUS, subject to the maximum payment at maturity.&#160;&#160;Under the terms of the Trigger PLUS, an investor would realize the maximum payment at maturity at a final index level of 112.75% of the initial index level<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, serif">.</font></font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">If the underlying index appreciates 3%, the investor would receive a 6% return, or $10.60 per Trigger PLUS.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">If the underlying index appreciates 20%, the investor would receive only the maximum payment at maturity of $12.55 per Trigger PLUS, or 125.50% of the stated principal amount.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Par Scenario.&#160;&#160;</font>If the final index level is less than or equal to the initial index level but is greater than or equal to the trigger level, investors would receive the stated principal amount of $10 per Trigger PLUS.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Downside Scenario.</font>&#160;&#160;If the final index level is less than the trigger level, the investor would receive an amount less than or equal to the $10 stated principal amount, based on a 1% loss of principal for each 1% decline in the underlying index.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 54pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline;" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">If the underlying index depreciates 30%, the investor would lose 30% of the investor&#8217;s principal and receive only $7.00 per Trigger PLUS at maturity, or 70% of the stated principal amount.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 8pt"><a name="mssbfooter"><!--efplaceholder--></a>September 2014</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 16pt"><a name="Risk_Factors"><!--EFPlaceholder--></a>Risk Factors</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">An investment in the Trigger PLUS is subject to the risks described below, as well as the risks described under &#8220;Risk Factors&#8221; in the accompanying prospectus supplement and prospectus. Investors in the Trigger PLUS are also exposed to further risks related to the issuer of the Trigger PLUS, Royal Bank of Canada, which are described in Royal Bank of Canada&#8217;s annual report on Form 40-F for the year ended October 31, 2013, filed with the SEC and incorporated by reference herein. See the categories of risks, identified and disclosed in the management&#8217;s discussion and analysis of financial condition and results of operations included in the annual report on Form 40-F. This section (and the management&#8217;s discussion and analysis section of the annual report on Form 40-F) describes the most significant risks relating to the Trigger PLUS. You should carefully consider whether the Trigger PLUS are suited to your particular circumstances.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The Trigger PLUS do not pay interest or guarantee return of any principal.</font>&#160;&#160;The terms of the Trigger PLUS differ from those of ordinary debt securities in that the Trigger PLUS do not pay interest or guarantee payment of the principal amount at maturity.&#160;&#160;If the final index level is less than the trigger level, you will lose some or all of your initial investment.&#160;&#160;Under these circumstances. the payout at maturity will be an amount in cash that is less than the $10 stated principal amount of each Trigger PLUS by an amount proportionate to the full decrease in the level of the underlying index<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, serif">.</font>&#160;&#160;There is no minimum payment at maturity of the Trigger PLUS, and you could lose your entire investment.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The appreciation potential of the Trigger PLUS is limited by the maximum payment at maturity.</font>&#160;&#160;The appreciation potential of the Trigger PLUS is limited by the maximum payment at maturity of $12.55 per Trigger PLUS, or 125.50% of the stated principal amount.&#160;&#160;Although the leverage factor provides 200% exposure to any increase in the level of the underlying index as of the valuation date above the initial index level, because the payment at maturity will be limited to 125.50% of the stated principal amount, any increase in the final index level over the initial index level by more than 12.75% will not further increase the return on the Trigger PLUS.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 11pt">Trigger PLUS Based on the Performance of the S&amp;P 500<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">&#174;</font> Index, due April 4, 2017</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #808080; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Trigger Performance Leveraged Upside Securities<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top">SM</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #808080; FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Principal at Risk Securities</font></div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The amount payable on the Trigger PLUS is not linked to the level of the underlying index at any time other than the valuation date.&#160;&#160;</font>The final index level will be based on the closing level of the underlying index on the valuation date, subject to adjustment for non-trading days and certain market disruption events.&#160;&#160;Even if the level of the underlying index appreciates prior to the valuation date but then decreases on the valuation date to a level that is less than the initial index level, the payment at maturity will be less, and may be significantly less, than it would have been had the payment at maturity been linked to the level of the underlying index prior to that decrease.&#160;&#160;Although the actual level of the underlying index on the maturity date or at other times during the term of the Trigger PLUS may be higher than the final index level, the payment at maturity will be based solely on the closing level of the underlying index on the valuation date.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Investing in the Trigger PLUS is not equivalent to investing in the underlying index.</font> Investing in the Trigger PLUS is not equivalent to investing in the underlying index or its component stocks. Investors in the Trigger PLUS will not have voting rights or rights to receive dividends or other distributions or any other rights with respect to stocks that constitute the underlying index.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div>
<table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="hangingindent" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">The initial estimated value of the Trigger PLUS is less than the price to the public.</font>&#160;&#160;The initial estimated value that is set forth on the cover page of this document does not represent a minimum price at which we, RBCCM or any of our affiliates would be willing to purchase the Trigger PLUS in any secondary market (if any exists) at any time.&#160;&#160;If you attempt to sell the Trigger PLUS prior to maturity, their market value may be lower than the price you paid for them and the initial estimated value.&#160;&#160;This is due to, among other things, changes in the level of the underlying index, the borrowing rate we pay to issue securities of this kind, and the inclusion in the price to the public of the agent&#8217;s commissions and the estimated costs relating to our hedging of the Trigger PLUS. These factors, together with various credit, market and economic factors over the term of the Trigger PLUS, are expected to reduce the price at which you may be able to sell the Trigger PLUS in any secondary market and will affect the value of the Trigger PLUS in complex and unpredictable ways.&#160;&#160;Assuming no change in market conditions or any other relevant factors, the price, if any, at which you may be able to sell your Trigger PLUS prior to maturity may be less than your original purchase price, as any such sale price would not be expected to include the agent&#8217;s commissions and the hedging costs relating to the Trigger PLUS<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, serif">.</font> In addition to bid-ask spreads, the value of the Trigger PLUS determined for any secondary market price is expected to be based on the secondary rate rather than the internal funding rate used to price the Trigger PLUS and determine the initial estimated value.&#160;&#160;As a result, the secondary price will be less than if the internal funding rate was used.&#160;&#160;The Trigger PLUS are not designed to be short-term trading instruments.&#160;&#160;Accordingly, you should be able and willing to hold your Trigger PLUS to maturity.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<tr valign="top">
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></div>
</td>
<td style="WIDTH: 18pt">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; COLOR: #a3c4eb; FONT-SIZE: 12pt" face="Wingdings">&#167;</font></font></div>
</td>
<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Our initial estimated value of the Trigger PLUS is an estimate only, calculated as of the pricing date</font>.&#160;&#160;The initial estimated value of the Trigger PLUS is based on the value of our obligation to make the payments on the Trigger PLUS, together with the mid-market value of the derivative embedded in the terms of the Trigger PLUS.&#160;&#160;See &#8220;Structuring the Trigger PLUS&#8221; below.&#160;&#160;Our estimate is based on a variety of assumptions, including our credit spreads, expectations as to dividends, interest rates and volatility, and the expected term of the Trigger PLUS.&#160;&#160;These assumptions are based on certain forecasts about future events, which may prove to be incorrect.&#160;&#160;Other entities may value the Trigger PLUS or similar securities at a price that is significantly different than we do.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The value of the Trigger PLUS at any time after the pricing date will vary based on many factors, including changes in market conditions, and cannot be predicted with accuracy.&#160;&#160;As a result, the actual value you would receive if you sold the Trigger PLUS in any secondary market, if any, should be expected to differ materially from the initial estimated value of your Trigger PLUS<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman, serif">.</font></font></div>

As a result, it is impossible to predict whether the level of the underlying index will rise or fall. Trading prices of the equity securities comprising the underlying index will be influenced by complex and interrelated political, economic, financial and other factors.</font></div>

<td>
<div align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Hedging and trading activity by us and our subsidiaries could potentially adversely affect the value of the Trigger PLUS.&#160;&#160;</font>One or more of our subsidiaries expect to carry out hedging activities related to the Trigger PLUS (and possibly to other instruments linked to the underlying index or the securities it represents), including trading in those securities as well as in other related instruments.&#160;&#160;Some of our subsidiaries also may conduct trading activities relating to the underlying index on a regular basis as part of their general broker-dealer and other businesses.&#160;&#160;Any of these hedging or trading activities on or prior to the pricing date could potentially have affected the initial index level and, therefore, could have increased the level at which the underlying index must close on the valuation date so that investors do not suffer a loss on their initial investment in the Trigger PLUS.&#160;&#160;Additionally, such hedging or trading activities during the term of the Trigger PLUS, including on the valuation date, could adversely affect the level of the underlying index on the valuation date and, accordingly, the amount of cash an investor will receive at maturi<font style="DISPLAY: inline">ty, if any.</font></font></div>

Neither we nor the agent have made any independent investigation regarding any matters whatsoever relating to the issuers of the securities represented by the underlying index.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The Internal Revenue Service has issued a notice indicating that it and the U.S. Treasury Department are actively considering whether, among other issues, a holder should be required to accrue interest over the term of an instrument such as the Trigger PLUS even though that holder will not receive any payments with respect to the Trigger PLUS until maturity and whether all or part of the gain a holder may recognize upon sale, exchange or maturity of an instrument such as the Trigger PLUS could be treated as ordinary income.&#160;&#160;The outcome of this process is uncertain and could apply on a retroactive basis.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Please read carefully the sections entitled &#8220;Canadian Federal Income Tax Consequences&#8221; and &#8220;Supplemental Discussion of U.S. Federal Income Tax Consequences&#8221; in this document, the section entitled &#8220;Tax Consequences&#8221; in the accompanying prospectus and the section entitled &#8220;Certain Income Tax Consequences&#8221; in the accompanying prospectus supplement.&#160;&#160;You should consult your tax advisor about your own tax situation.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" width="100%" style="FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: arial">
<tr bgcolor="#296dc1">
<td align="left" colspan="2" valign="middle" width="86%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; COLOR: #ffffff; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Additional Provisions</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr bgcolor="#dcebf4">
<td align="left" valign="top" width="22%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial bold, times new roman, serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Postponement of the</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial bold, times new roman, serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">valuation date:</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="65%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">If the valuation date occurs on a day that is not a trading day or on a day on which the calculation agent has determined that a market disruption event (as defined below) has occurred or is continuing, then the valuation date will be postponed until the next succeeding trading day on which the calculation agent determines that a market disruption event does not occur or is not continuing; provided that in no event will the valuation date be postponed by more than five trading days. If the valuation date is postponed by five trading days, and a market disruption event occurs or is continuing on that fifth trading day, then the calculation agent may determine, in its good faith and reasonable judgment, what the closing level of the underlying index would have been in the absence of the market disruption event.&#160;&#160;&#160;If the valuation date is postponed, then the maturity date will be postponed by an equal number of business days. No interest shall accrue or be payable as a result of such postponement.</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr bgcolor="#dcebf4">
<td valign="top" width="22%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td valign="middle" width="65%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
</tr><tr>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="22%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Market disruption events:</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="65%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">With respect to the underlying index and any relevant successor index, a &#8220;market disruption event&#8221; means:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a suspension, absence or material limitation of trading of equity securities then constituting 20% or more of the level of the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) on the relevant exchanges (as defined below) for such securities for more than two hours of trading during, or during the one hour period preceding the close of, the principal trading session on such relevant exchange; or</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a breakdown or failure in the price and trade reporting systems of any relevant exchange as a result of which the reported trading prices for equity securities then constituting 20% or more of the level of the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) during the one hour preceding the close of the principal trading session on such relevant exchange are materially inaccurate; or</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a suspension, absence or material limitation of trading on the primary exchange or market for trading in futures or options contracts related to the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) for more than two hours of trading during, or during the one hour period preceding the close of, the principal trading session on such exchange or market; or</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a decision to permanently discontinue trading in the relevant futures or options contracts;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">in each case as determined by the calculation agent in its sole discretion; and</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a determination by the calculation agent in its sole discretion that the event described above materially interfered with our ability or the ability of any of our affiliates to adjust or unwind all or a material portion of any hedge with respect to the Trigger PLUS.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">For purposes of determining whether a market disruption event with respect to the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) exists at any time, if trading in a security included in the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) is materially suspended or materially limited at that time, then the relevant percentage contribution of that security to the level of the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) will be based on a comparison of (a) the portion of the level of the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) attributable to that security relative to (b) the overall level of the underlying index (or the relevant successor index), in each case immediately before that suspension or limitation.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<td valign="top" width="22%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="65%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">For purposes of determining whether a market disruption event with respect to the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) has occurred:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a limitation on the hours or number of days of trading will not constitute a market disruption event if it results from an announced change in the regular business hours of the relevant exchange, or the primary exchange or market for trading in futures or options contracts related to the underlying index (or the relevant successor index);</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>limitations pursuant to the rules of any relevant exchange similar to NYSE Rule 80B (or any applicable rule or regulation enacted or promulgated by any other self-regulatory organization or any government agency of scope similar to NYSE Rule 80B as determined by the calculation agent) on trading during significant market fluctuations will constitute a suspension, absence or material limitation of trading;</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 54pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a suspension of trading in futures or options contracts on the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) by the primary exchange or market trading in such contracts by reason of:</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a price change exceeding limits set by such exchange or market,</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>an imbalance of orders relating to such contracts, or</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a disparity in bid and ask quotes relating to such contracts<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman, serif">,</font></font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">will, in each such case, constitute a suspension, absence or material limitation of trading in futures or options contracts related to the underlying index (or the relevant successor index); and</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: -18pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: symbol, serif">&#183;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>a &#8220;suspension, absence or material limitation of trading&#8221; on any relevant exchange or on the primary exchange or market on which futures or options contracts related to the underlying index (or the relevant successor index) are traded will not include any time when such exchange or market is itself closed for trading under ordinary circumstances.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#8220;Relevant exchange&#8221; means the primary exchange or market of trading for any security (or any combination thereof) then included in the underlying index or such successor index, as applicable.</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr>
<td valign="top" width="22%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td valign="middle" width="65%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
</tr><tr bgcolor="#dcebf4">
<td align="left" valign="top" width="22%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Discontinuation </font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">of/adjustments to the </font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; COLOR: #296dc1; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">underlying index:</font></div>
</td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="65%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">If the index sponsor discontinues publication of the underlying index and the index sponsor or another entity publishes a successor or substitute index that the calculation agent determines, in its sole discretion, to be comparable to the discontinued index (such index being referred to herein as a &#8220;successor index&#8221;), then the closing level of the underlying index on the valuation date will be determined by reference to the level of such successor index at the close of trading on the relevant exchange for the successor index on such day.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Upon any selection by the calculation agent of a successor index, the calculation agent will cause written notice to be promptly furnished to the trustee, to us and to the holders of the Trigger PLUS.</font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>

<td valign="top" width="22%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>
<td align="left" valign="middle" width="65%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">If the index sponsor discontinues publication of the underlying index prior to, and that discontinuation is continuing on the valuation date, and the calculation agent determines, in its sole discretion, that no successor index is available at that time or the calculation agent has previously selected a successor index and publication of that successor index is discontinued prior to, and that discontinuation is continuing on, the valuation date, then the calculation agent will determine the closing level of the underlying index for that date.&#160;&#160;The closing level of the underlying index will be computed by the calculation agent in accordance with the formula for and method of calculating the underlying index or successor index, as applicable, last in effect prior to the discontinuation, using the closing price (or, if trading in the relevant securities has been materially suspended or materially limited, the calculation agent&#8217;s good faith estimate of the closing price that would have prevailed but for the suspension or limitation) at the close of the principal trading session on that date of each security most recently included in the underlying index or successor index, as applicable.</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">If at any time the method of calculating the underlying index or a successor index, or the level thereof, is changed in a material respect, or if the underlying index or a successor index is in any other way modified so that the underlying index or successor index does not, in the opinion of the calculation agent, fairly represent the level of the underlying index or successor index had those changes or modifications not been made, then the calculation agent will, at the close of business in New York City on the date on which the closing level of the underlying index is to be determined, make any calculations and adjustments as, in the good faith judgment of the calculation agent, may be necessary in order to arrive at a level of a stock index comparable to the underlying index or successor index, as the case may be, as if those changes or modifications had not been made, and calculate the closing level of the underlying index with reference to the underlying index or such successor index, as adjusted.&#160;&#160;Accordingly, if the method of calculating the underlying index or a successor index is modified so that the level of the underlying index or such successor index is a fraction of what it would have been if there had been no such modification (e.g., due to a split in the underlying index), then the calculation agent will adjust its calculation of the underlying index or such successor index in order to arrive at a level of the underlying index or such successor index as if there had been no such modification (e.g., as if such split had not occurred).</font></div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Notwithstanding these alternative arrangements, discontinuation the publication of or modification of the underlying index or successor index, as applicable, may adversely affect the value of the Trigger PLUS.</font></div>

</td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="65%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">A business day means a Monday, Tuesday, Wednesday, Thursday or Friday that is not a day on which banking institutions in The City of New York generally are authorized or obligated by law, regulation or executive order to close.</font></div>
</td>
</tr><tr bgcolor="#ffffff">
<td valign="top" width="22%"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; </font></td>

</td>
<td align="left" valign="top" width="65%">
<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: arial, sans-serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The trading day means a day, as determined by the calculation agent, on which trading is generally conducted on (i) the relevant exchanges for securities comprising the underlying index or the successor index and (ii) the exchanges on which futures or options contracts related to the underlying index or the successor index are traded, other than a day on which trading on such relevant exchange or exchange on which such futures or options contracts are traded is scheduled to close prior to its regular weekday closing time.</font></div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-SIZE: 8pt">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
